## [Shane Davis](http://www.comicvine.com/shane-davis/26-42742/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/40/2386608-shanedavis_564_icon.jpeg" align="right" /> ##

## [Greg Espinoza](http://www.comicvine.com/greg-espinoza/26-59646/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/7/71952/1316002-gregespinoza_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Greg Espinoza is a comic book artist who has worked for multiple comic book publishers such as Blackthorne, TSR, Malibu, Eclipse, and Antarctic Press among others.

* [Cherry's Jubilee (1992)](http://www.comicvine.com/cherrys-jubilee/49-34895/) 1 (artist)
* [Pug (2010)](http://www.comicvine.com/pug/49-34456/) 1 (artist)


## [David Finch](http://www.comicvine.com/david-finch/26-3226/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/40/2386544-davidfinch_564_icon.jpeg" align="right" /> ##
David Finch is a comic book artist/writer born in Canada. He has taken on his own series Batman: The Dark Knight where is writing and penciling but is known for his monumental covers such as Action Comics #900.

* [100% Marvel (2003)](http://www.comicvine.com/100-marvel/49-40653/) 33 (cover)
* [5 Days To Die (2010)](http://www.comicvine.com/5-days-to-die/49-35351/) 1 (cover)

* [Alan Moore's Glory (2001)](http://www.comicvine.com/alan-moores-glory/49-20413/) 1 (cover)
* [Alan Moore's Glory Preview (2001)](http://www.comicvine.com/alan-moores-glory-preview/49-38197/) 1 (artist)
* [All-New Official Handbook Of The Marvel Universe A To Z (2006)](http://www.comicvine.com/all-new-official-handbook-of-the-marvel-universe-a-to-z/49-18126/) 11 (artist)
* [All-New Official Handbook Of The Marvel Universe A To Z: Update (2007)](http://www.comicvine.com/all-new-official-handbook-of-the-marvel-universe-a-to-z-update/49-18224/) 2 (penciler)
* [Aphrodite IX (2000)](http://www.comicvine.com/aphrodite-ix/49-18912/) 0 (artist, cover, penciler, writer)
* [Arcanum (1997)](http://www.comicvine.com/arcanum/49-6085/) 2 (cover)

## [Tess Fowler](http://www.comicvine.com/tess-fowler/26-58976/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/62766/1167293-tess_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Tess Fowler is a comic book illustrator based in California. To date she has worked on Michelle Obama Year One, Wonderland Annual 2010, Grimm Fairy Tales #54 and Charmed Issue #6. Her credits also include Heavy Metal Magazine and multiple sketch card projects. www.tessfowler.com

* [Charmed (2010)](http://www.comicvine.com/charmed/49-32132/) 6, 11, 19 (artist, penciler)
* [Charmed Season Nine (2011)](http://www.comicvine.com/charmed-season-nine/49-38879/) 2 (artist, penciler)
* [Female Force: Michelle Obama: Year One (2010)](http://www.comicvine.com/female-force-michelle-obama-year-one/49-32223/) 1 (penciler)
* [Grimm Fairy Tales (2005)](http://www.comicvine.com/grimm-fairy-tales/49-19824/) 54 (penciler)

## [Ramona Fradon](http://www.comicvine.com/ramona-fradon/26-33524/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/2/24461/432629-ramona_fradon_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Under appreciated female pioneer artist in the male dominated comic book industry.  The first female to draw Superheroes in comic books!  Ms. Fradon worked on Aquaman & is credited as co-creator of Metamorpho. Working through the Golden, Silver, Bronze and Modern-Age of comics.

* [100-Page Super Spectacular (1973)](http://www.comicvine.com/100-page-super-spectacular/49-2606/) 15 (inker, penciler)

## [Agnes Garbowska](http://www.comicvine.com/agnes-garbowska/26-58854/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/40/2000131-photo_on_2011_09_06_at_21_icon.jpeg" align="right" /> ##
Freelance artist, who lives in Toronto, Ontario, Canada. Agnes Garbowska was born in Poland and came to Canada when she was four years old. Being an only child she escaped into a world of books, cartoons, and comics.

## [Stan Goldberg](http://www.comicvine.com/stan-goldberg/26-9681/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/69676/1601197-stan_goldberg_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Stan Goldberg is a long time artist for Archie Comics.  He is also well known for Millie the Model.  He famously worked on Fantastic Four #1 as well.  He is a creator who has well over 3,000 issues under his belt!

## [Keron Grant](http://www.comicvine.com/keron-grant/26-42893/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/77/238042-155949-keron-grant_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##

* [Action Comics (1938)](http://www.comicvine.com/action-comics/49-18005/) 790 (penciler)

## [Larry Hama](http://www.comicvine.com/larry-hama/26-12272/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/5/52043/1314420-450px_larryhama5.23.09byluiginovi_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Larry Hama is a comic book writer with numerous credits, notably in the titles Wolverine, Venom Finale, Nth Man the Ultimate Ninja, and both G.I. Joe: A Real American Hero and its spin-off G.I. Joe: Special Missions.

## [Rob Liefeld](http://www.comicvine.com/rob-liefeld/26-5181/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/2493/98692-14213-rob-liefeld_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Rob Liefeld is a comic book penciller, writer, and creator who rose to record-breaking success in the 1990's with titles such as The New Mutants, X-Force, and Youngblood. Mr. Liefeld is truly a prolific talent, and in many ways represents everything that is wrong with comics today.

## [Francis Manapul](http://www.comicvine.com/francis-manapul/26-7685/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/5/56507/2008396-francis_icon.png" align="right" /> ##

## [Bill Maus](http://www.comicvine.com/bill-maus/26-49184/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/1/15238/1271431-bill_maus_02_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Bill Maus is an independent small press comic book artist/ creator best known for his run on Zen: Intergalactic Ninja, Nira-X: Cyberangel and The Skunk for Comic Book publishers such as Avatar Press, Zen Comics, Entity Comics and many more.

## [Danny Miki](http://www.comicvine.com/danny-miki/26-1922/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/229/118095-190094-danny-miki_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Danny Miki is one the best inker still to date. His work spans from Marvel, DC, and Image comics. Married to the Etreme Studios receptionist during the late 90's.

* [Absolute Superman for Tomorrow (2009)](http://www.comicvine.com/absolute-superman-for-tomorrow/49-37755/) 1 (inker)

## [Jeffrey Moy](http://www.comicvine.com/jeffrey-moy/26-1515/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/77/254670-103424-jeffrey-moy_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##

## [Todd Nauck](http://www.comicvine.com/todd-nauck/26-9641/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/64507/2271591-todd_nauck_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Todd's been drawing comics since the early 90s and has published work with all the major companies including Marvel, DC, Dark Horse, and Image.  He currently is drawing Friendly Neighborhood Spidey.

## [Wendy Pini](http://www.comicvine.com/wendy-pini/26-1547/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/40/726849-pini_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##

## [Whilce Portacio](http://www.comicvine.com/whilce-portacio/26-6024/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/64507/2070498-whilce_portacio_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Filipino/American Comic book artist who has worked for Marvel, DC, and Image. Portacio was one of the original 7 founders of Image Comics.   He is also the creator of a number of big characters-including the X-men favorite Bishop.

## [Livio Ramondelli](http://www.comicvine.com/livio-ramondelli/26-58322/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/9055/1039419-green_lantern_by_livio27_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Livio Ramondelli is a concept artist who currently works for DC/Wildstorm. Although he is a penciler he is known to often use paints and pastels for finished pieces.

## [Herb Trimpe](http://www.comicvine.com/herb-trimpe/26-3439/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/229/98810-67196-herb-trimpe_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Herb Trimpe is known for his long run in the hulk issues 106-193 and being the co-creator of wolverine although according to herb he did not help making wolverine he just "brought him to life".  He currently takes on occational projects for various publishers.

## [Michael E. Uslan](http://www.comicvine.com/michael-e-uslan/26-61509/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/61822/1840101-michaeluslan_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Born and raised in New Jersey, Michael Uslan was a comic book fan from an early age. In college, he made history by starting the first accredited course on comic book history. He later succeeded in Hollywood by producing such films as "Swamp Thing" and the Batman films. 

* [America at War: The Best of DC War Comics (1979)](http://www.comicvine.com/america-at-war-the-best-of-dc-war-comics/49-41512/) 1 (writer)

## [John Van Fleet](http://www.comicvine.com/john-van-fleet/26-26140/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/64507/2082359-john_van_fleet_icon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
